# Words that extend the spell checker. See ignore.txt for words that should be
# completely ignored (i.e. not used to create suggestions).
# Hyphenated compound words containing words listed here will be accepted, too:
# If this file contains "Au-pair", then "Au-pair-Agentur" will not be marked as incorrect.
# Compound words starting with words listed here will be accepted, too:
# If this file contains "Secondhand" or "Helizität", then "Secondhandladen"
#  or "Helizitätsoperator" will not be marked as incorrect.
# (For words ending with "tum", "ling", "ion", "tät", "keit", "schaft", "sicht", "ung", or "en"
#  a Fugen-S will be inserted internally, such as in 'HelizitätSoperator')
# Supported suffixes for German:
# /E will add e
# /S will add s
# /N will add n
# /A will add e, er, es, en, em (for adjectives - no comparative, no superlative)
#             if the word already ends in 'e', only r, s, n, m will be added
# /F will add in (for gendered nouns)
# Use `prefix_verb` to prepend the given prefix to all forms of the verb (does not work for verbs with "ß" yet).
# Use `\_` to add words with an underscore.
# Words ending in `_in` will be expanded to have the common gender gap characters: $1*in, $1:in, $1_in, $1*innen, $1:innen, $1_innen
# The lines in `prefix_verb` syntax will also be used by GermanTagger.
